    $(function(){
         var urlUtenti='http://utenti.crol.it/';        
                     
             if( $('iframe[src*="www.informa-"]').length>0 ){ 
                 
                 $.ajax({
                     url:' custom_widget/registrazione.jsp',
                     data: {isLogged:''},
                     dataType: 'json',
                     success: function(response){
                         
                         var vars = [], hash;
                                 var q = document.URL.split('?')[1];
                                 if(q != undefined){
                                     q = q.split('&');
                                     for(var i = 0; i < q.length; i++){
                                         hash = q[i].split('=');
                                         vars.push(hash[1]);
                                         vars[hash[0]] = hash[1];
                                     }
                             }
                             var param_informa='';
                             if(typeof(vars['id_informa']) != 'undefined'){
                                 param_informa="id="+vars['id_informa'];
                             }
                         
                         if(response.logged){
                             $('iframe[src*="www.informa-"]').each(function(){
                                 $(this).attr('src', $(this).attr('src')+'?ID_utente='+response.ID_Utente+'&codiceControllo='+response.CodiceControllo+(param_informa!=''?'&'+param_informa:'') );
                             });
                         }else if(param_informa != ''){
                             $('iframe[src*="www.informa-"]').each(function(){
                                 $(this).attr('src', $(this).attr('src')+'?'+param_informa );
                             });
                         }
                     }
                 });
             }
             function register(){
                 var _this=$(this);
                 $.ajax({
                     url:'custom_widget/registrazione.jsp',
                     data: {isLogged:''},
                     dataType: 'json',
                     success: function(response){
                         $('#form_registrati').remove()
                         $('body').append('<form id="form_registrati"></form>');                        
                         var form = $('#form_registrati').attr('action', urlUtenti+'registrazione.aspx').attr('method','post');
                         form.append('<input type="hidden" name="urlRitorno" value="'+window.location.href+'" />');                        
                         if(response.logged){
                             form.append('<input type="hidden" name="ID_Utente" value="'+response.ID_Utente+'" />');
                             form.append('<input type="hidden" name="codiceControllo" value="'+response.CodiceControllo+'" />');
                             form.append('<input type="hidden" name="ID_Servizio" value="'+response.IdProfiloUtente+'" />');
                         }else{
                             form.append('<input type="hidden" name="ID_Utente" value="" />');
                             if(_this.parent().parent().hasClass('login_incolonna')){
                                 form.append('<input type="hidden" name="ID_Servizio" value="1" />');
                             }else{
                                 form.append('<input type="hidden" name="ID_Servizio" value="3" />');
                             }
                         }                                                
                         form.submit();                        
                     }                    
                 });      
             }
             if(location.href.indexOf('/registrati')!=-1){
                 register();
             }
             $(document).on('click','a[href*="registrati"]',function(e){
                 e.preventDefault();
                 register();
                 return false;
             });
             
             $(document).on('click','.ApriPassword, .password_dimenticata',function(){                
                 $('.recupera_password').remove();
                 $('.recupera_password_commenti').remove();
                 $('#form_registrati').remove()                
                 $('body').append('<form id="form_registrati"></form>');                
                 var form = $('#form_registrati').attr('action', urlUtenti+'recuperoPwd.aspx').attr('method','post').attr('target','_blank');
                 form.append('<input type="hidden" name="urlRitorno" value="'+window.location.href+'" />');                
                 form.submit();
                 window.setTimeout(function(){location.reload();},1000);
                 return false;
             })            
         
     });
   </script>

     function search_reset_fields(element){
           $("#"+element+" form").get(0).reset();
           $("#"+element+" form").find("input[type=text]").val("");
           $("#"+element+" form").find("select").val("");
           $("#"+element+" form").find('.label_checkbox.checked').removeClass('checked');
     }

         $('.menu_2 li').mouseover(function(e){
                                             var father=$(this);
                                             var sottomenu=father.find('.menu_3');
                                             if(!sottomenu.hasClass('calcolato')){ // ancora non ho fatto il calcolo
                                                     sottomenu.addClass('menuL');
                                                     var container=$('#container');
                                                     var margineSinistro=e.pageX; // IE 8 non supporta offset, quindi prendo la posizione del mouse
                                                     var wBox=sottomenu.outerWidth(); //la width deve essere specificata nel CSS
                                                     var margineDxBox=margineSinistro+wBox;
                                                     var margineDxContainer=document.getElementById("container").offsetLeft+container.outerWidth(); // uso getElementById per l'offset per IE8
                                                     if(margineDxBox>margineDxContainer){
                                                             sottomenu.removeClass('menuL').addClass('menuR');
                                                     }else{
                                                     }
                                                     sottomenu.addClass('calcolato');
                                             }
                                     });
        </script>
